<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:spier.html>spier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pointed.html>pointed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:object.html>object</a>; <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spīker</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spīkāri</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*spīkārī</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>Late</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spīcārium</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Speicher</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saxon.html>Saxon</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">spīkari</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spikkels.html>spikkels</a> (99538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spiritueel.html>spiritueel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-iteit</i>

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">spirituality</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Danish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-oda">splittæ</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:splitten.html>splitten</a></i>.
